async function checkUrl1(url){
 const res = await fetch(url);
 const html = await res.text();
 const text = html.replace(/<script[\s\S]*?<\/script>/gi,' ').replace(/<style[\s\S]*?<\/style>/gi,' ').replace(/<[^>]+>/g,' ').replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim();
 const idx = text.indexOf('Home Type');
 const title = (text.match(/\$[0-9,]+.*?Total Monthly Price.*?([0-9]+ Beds?.*?sq ft)/) || [])[0];
 return {url, status: res.status, homeSnippet: idx>=0? text.slice(idx, idx+250): '', titleSnippet: text.slice(0,200), hasCondo: /Home Type\s+Condo/.test(text), available: (text.match(/Available\s+(Available Now|[A-Za-z]+ \d+)/)||[])[0]};
}
